(macro:...any-type _i,[(output:)[(if:$Status contains (dm:"胀",100))[(set:$food to 60)](else:)[(set:$food to it + _i's 1st)(if:$food > 100)[(set:$food to 100)](else-if:$food < 1)[(set:$food to 0)](rerun:?top)(append:?eventsBox)[(if:$food <30)[<br>$box[你感觉肚子有点饿......]]]]]]) ) <!--饱腹快捷宏 END--> <!--健康快捷宏--> (set:$health_add to (macro:...any-type _i,[(output:)[(set:$health to it + _i's (set:$san_add to (macro:...any-type _i,[(output:)[(set:$san to it + _i's 1st)(if:$san > 100)[(set:$san to 100)](else-if:$san < 1)[(set:$san to 0)](rerun:?top)(append:?eventsBox)[(if:$san <30)[<br>$box[你感觉自己快要崩溃了......]]]]]) ) <!--理智快捷宏 END--> <!--数值通用快捷宏--> (set:$add to (macro:...any-type _i,[(output:)[(set:_i's 1st to it + _i's 2nd)(if:_i's 1s > 100)[(set:_i's 1s to 100)](else-if:_i's 1st < 1)[(set:_i's 1st to 0)](rerun:?top)(append:?eventsBox)[(if:_i's 1st >0)[<br>$box[(print:_i's 1st)&ensp;(print:_i's 2nd)&emsp;]]]]]) ) <!--数值通用快捷宏END--> <!--时间快捷宏-->
